<path>E:\Projects\shiftplan-generator\README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: # ShiftPlan Generator — Sistem Jadwal Security
2: 
3: Aplikasi web untuk mengelola dan menghasilkan jadwal shift 12 jam (Pagi & Malam) Security Yayasan Ganesa Satria Temanggung / SMK Ganesa Satria 4 Kedu.
4: 
5: ## Fitur
6: 
7: - **Generate Jadwal Otomatis** — Algoritma cerdas untuk penjadwalan shift pagi & malam dengan aturan operasional (max hari beruntun, preferensi shift, dll)
8: - **Aturan Khusus Hari** — Kuota pagi berkurang di akhir pekan, pembagian shift pendek/penuh di hari Jumat
9: - **Panel Dashboard** — Widget informasi karyawan, status pengamanan pos, arsip bulan
10: - **Edit Manual** — Klik sel jadwal untuk mengubah shift secara manual
11: - **Manajemen Karyawan** — Tambah, edit, dan hapus data personil
12: - **Ekspor PDF** — Download jadwal ke PDF siap cetak
13: - **Penyimpanan Lokal** — Data tersimpan otomatis di browser (localStorage)
14: 
15: ## Teknologi
16: 
17: - React 18 (CDN via UMD)
18: - Tailwind CSS (CDN)
19: - Lucide Icons
20: - jsPDF + jspdf-autotable
21: - Babel Standalone
22: 
23: ## Cara Pakai
24: 
25: 1. Buka `index.html` di browser (atau jalankan via live server)
26: 2. Tambah data karyawan di tab **Kelola Karyawan**
27: 3. Pilih bulan/tahun, klik **Generate Jadwal**
28: 4. Edit shift manual jika perlu (klik sel jadwal)
29: 5. Ekspor ke PDF atau cetak langsung
30: 
31: ## Struktur
32: 
33: ```
34: index.html        — Aplikasi single-page (semua dalam satu file)
35: opencode.json     — Konfigurasi OpenCode
36: .cac/             — Auto-commit hooks (code-agent-auto-commit)
37: README.md         — Dokumentasi ini
38: ```
39: 
40: ## Lisensi
41: 
42: MIT

(End of file - total 42 lines)
</content>
```

## Summary of PDF Export Functionality

The entire application is a **single-page application** contained in one file (`index.html`), which includes all PDF generation logic inline. There are no separate component or utility files -- the PDF export is implemented directly within the HTML via embedded JavaScript using **jsPDF** and **jspdf-autotable**.

---

51: This is a **purely client-side (frontend-only)** web application. There is **no backend server, no runtime, and no build step**.

53: - **JavaScript (vanilla, no TypeScript)** -- All application logic is written in plain JavaScript with JSX syntax.
54: - **React 18** -- Loaded via CDN as UMD bundles (`react.production.min.js`, `react-dom.production.min.js`) from `unpkg.com`. No npm/webpack/vite build chain.
55: - **Babel Standalone** -- Loaded via CDN (`@babel/standalone/babel.min.js`) to transpile JSX in the browser at runtime.
56: - **Tailwind CSS** -- Loaded via CDN (`cdn.tailwindcss.com`). The in-browser Tailwind engine is configured via `tailwind.config` in a `<script>` block.
57: - **jsPDF + jspdf-autotable** -- For PDF export, loaded via CDN (`cdnjs.cloudflare.com`).
58: - **Lucide Icons** -- Loaded via CDN (`unpkg.com/lucide@latest`).
59: - **canvas-confetti** -- For celebration effects, loaded via CDN (`cdn.jsdelivr.net`).
60: - **Google Fonts (Inter)** -- Loaded via Google Fonts API.

79: ## 3. Framework
80: 
81: - **React 18** -- The UI framework.
82: - **Tailwind CSS** -- The styling framework (used via CDN's in-browser engine).
83: - **No build framework** (no Vite, Webpack, Next.js, Gatsby, etc.)
84: 
85: The application uses `React.createElement` / JSX (transpiled in-browser by Babel Standalone). All state is managed via React hooks (`useState`, `useEffect`, `useMemo`).
86: 
87: ---
88: 
89: ## 4. Full-Stack App?
90: 
91: **No.** This is a **frontend-only single-page application (SPA)**. There is:
92: 
93: - No backend server
94: - No API routes
95: - No database connection
96: - No authentication system
97: - No build step
98: 
99: All data persistence is done via the **browser's `localStorage` API**. Employee data and schedules are stored as JSON strings in `localStorage` under the keys `gs_employees` and `gs_all_schedules`.
100: 
101: ---
102: 
103: ## 5. Docker Configuration
104: 
105: **No Dockerfile or docker-compose file exists anywhere in the project.**
106: 
107: ---
108: 
109: ## 6. Database Configuration
110: 
111: **No database configuration exists.** The app uses **client-side `localStorage`** only. There are:
112: 
113: - No SQLite files
114: - No PostgreSQL/MySQL connection strings
115: - No ORM config
116: - No `.env` database variables for the app (the `.cac/.env.example` file is for the auto-commit AI tooling, not the app)
117: 
118: ---
119: 
120: ## 7. How the App is Started
121: 
122: Since there is no server or build step, the app is started by simply opening the HTML file in a web browser:
123: 
124: ```
125: Simply open:  E:\Projects\shiftplan-generator\index.html
126: ```
127: 
128: Or serve it with any static file server, for example:
129: - **VS Code Live Server** extension (right-click `index.html` -> "Open with Live Server")
130: - `npx serve .` (if Node.js is available)
131: - `python -m http.server` (if Python is available)
132: - Any HTTP server of your choice
133: 
134: There are **no npm scripts** (`start`, `dev`, `build`) because there is no `package.json` at the project root.
135: 
136: ---
137: 
138: ## 8. Project Structure (Key Directories)
139: 
140: ```
141: E:\Projects\shiftplan-generator\
142: ├── index.html                  ★ THE ENTIRE APPLICATION (single-file SPA)
143: ├── README.md                   Project documentation
144: ├── opencode.json               OpenCode AI assistant config
145: │
146: ├── .cac/                       Code-agent auto-commit tooling (local AI helper)
147: │   ├── .code-agent-auto-commit.json   Auto-commit configuration
148: │   ├── .env.example                  Example API keys for AI providers
149: │   ├── .env                          (actual API keys, gitignored)
150: │   └── run-*.log                     Auto-commit run logs
151: │
152: ├── .opencode/                  OpenCode AI plugin system
153: │   ├── package.json            OpenCode plugin dependencies
154: │   ├── package-lock.json
155: │   ├── .gitignore              Ignores node_modules etc.
156: │   ├── node_modules/           Installed plugin deps (zod, uuid, etc.)
157: │   └── plugins/
158: │       └── code-agent-auto-commit.ts   Auto-commit plugin source
159: │
160: ├── .git/                       Git repository data
161: │
162: └── conversations/              (empty) Auto-saved conversation history folder
163: ```
164: 
165: ---
166: 
167: ## Key Observations for Deployment
168: 
169: 1. **Deployment is trivial** -- This is a static site. Upload `index.html` and `README.md` to any static host (Netlify, Vercel, GitHub Pages, S3, Nginx, Apache) or attach it to an email.
170: 
171: 2. **No server-side processing** -- All data lives in the user's browser. Different browsers/devices do not share data.
172: 
173: 3. **No build step required** -- The file is ready to serve as-is.
174: 
175: 4. **Dependencies are all CDN** -- No local `node_modules` are needed for the app to function. The `.opencode/node_modules/` directory is for the OpenCode tooling only and is not part of the application.
176: 
177: 5. **No environment variables** -- The `.cac/.env` file is for the AI auto-commit tool, not for the application.
178: </task_result>
179: </task>
180: ```

---

## COMPLETE DEPLOYMENT FINDINGS

### 1. THE `.cac/` DIRECTORY CONTENTS

The `.cac/` directory contains **code-agent-auto-commit tooling** -- a local AI-powered auto-commit and auto-push agent. It has the following files:

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `.code-agent-auto-commit.json` | **Main config** -- defines auto-commit behavior |
| `.env` | API keys for AI providers (gitignored, currently empty) |
| `.env.example` | Template for the env file |
| `run-*.log` (25 log files) | Run logs from the auto-commit agent, all dated 2026-06-05 |

**The critical file is `.code-agent-auto-commit.json`** (`E:\Projects\shiftplan-generator\.cac\.code-agent-auto-commit.json`). It contains:

- **`push.enabled: true`** -- auto-push is enabled
- **`push.provider: "github"`** -- pushes to GitHub
- **`push.remote: "origin"`** -- uses the `origin` remote
- **`push.branch: "main"`** -- configured to push to the `main` branch
- **`commit.mode: "single"`** -- commits changes as a single commit
- **`commit.fallbackPrefix: "chore(auto)"`** -- commit message prefix

**Critical issue:** The agent is configured to push to `main`, but the local repository only has a `master` branch (no `main` branch exists locally). Every single log file (all 25 of them) contains **the same error**:

```
Error: git -C E:\Projects\shiftplan-generator push origin main failed:
error: src refspec main does not match any
error: failed to push some refs to 'https://github.com/addiarifianto/shiftplan-generator.git'
```

This means **the auto-push has never succeeded**. The auto-commit agent has been trying to push every few minutes throughout the day (from 07:21 to 21:34 UTC), but all pushes fail because it targets `main` while the branch is named `master`.

---

**No git hooks exist.** The `.git/hooks/` directory has no custom hooks, and `core.hooksPath` is not configured. There is no mechanism for auto-deploy triggered by local commits.

### 5. CAC-RELATED CONFIGURATION SUMMARY

**What is `.cac/`?**
It is the working directory for a tool called **"code-agent-auto-commit"** (implemented as an OpenCode plugin at `.opencode/plugins/code-agent-auto-commit.ts`). This tool:

- Watches for file changes in the project
- Uses AI to generate commit messages (configured AI providers: OpenAI, Anthropic, Moonshot, Minimax, Ollama)
- Auto-commits changes
- **Attempts to auto-push** to GitHub (but fails due to branch name mismatch: configured for `main`, but the repo uses `master`)

---

### 6. CURRENT DEPLOYMENT STATUS (VERIFIED LIVE)

- **URL:** `https://shiftplan-generator.vercel.app/` -- **IS LIVE AND RESPONDING**
- The site returned: "Sistem Jadwal Security Ganesa Satria" (verified healthy)
- **Deployment method:** Vercel web dashboard (GitHub integration), set up manually by the user
- **Auto-deploy:** Vercel's GitHub integration automatically redeploys when code is pushed to the GitHub repo. HOWEVER, because the auto-commit agent's push to `main` fails, and manual `git push` has not been done for recent commits, **the live site may be behind the local code**.
- **Branch situation:** Local branch is `master`, remote origin branch is `origin/master`. The auto-commit agent tries `main` which doesn't exist.
- **GitHub repo:** `https://github.com/addiarifianto/shiftplan-generator` (git remote: `origin`)
- **Quick fix needed:** Either rename `master` to `main` locally (`git branch -m master main`) and push, or update `.cac/.code-agent-auto-commit.json` to set `push.branch` to `"master"`.
